[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA libFuzzer run on the PDF text-extraction harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`PDFExtractTextFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mterminated with a timeout error. The fuzzer’s main thread remained in a RUNNABLE [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstate for over [0m[1;36m28[0m[39m seconds, repeatedly executing into the Apache FontBox/Type1 font [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsing code [0m[1;39m([0m[39mspecifically `Type1Parser.readEncoding` → `Type1Parser.parseASCII` → [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Type1Parser.parse`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which stalled the fuzz target. No crash or exception is [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreported—only a fuzzer timeout indicating a potential hang or extremely slow [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsing path.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- What the issue is  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The libFuzzer driver aborted after exceeding its execution time limit [0m[1;39m([0m[39m“ERROR: [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibFuzzer: timeout”[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The attached thread dump shows that the fuzzer’s main thread [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis stuck in the PDF parsing pipeline, never completing the call to [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`fuzzerTestOneInput`. There is no sign of an OOM, crash, or exception; instead, the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode appears to enter a prolonged or infinite loop when processing certain inputs.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  While not explicitly labeled in the report, this condition constitutes a [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDenial-of-Service [0m[1;39m([0m[39mDoS[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m or “hang” vulnerability: a specially crafted PDF input can [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcause the parser to stall indefinitely, preventing progress and exhausting fuzzing [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresources.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Important observations and findings  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The main thread is repeatedly invoking native instrumentation [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`TraceDataFlowNativeCallbacks.traceConstCmpInt`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m before falling into the FontBox [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mType1 parsing routines.  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The hang occurs during font parsing steps:  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – `Type1Parser.readEncoding` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m217[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – `Type1Parser.parseASCII` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m142[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – `Type1Parser.parse` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m63[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Downstream calls include creation of `Type1Font` with a PFB stream, [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minitialization of `PDType1Font`, and eventual text-extraction via [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`PDFTextStripper`.  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • No other threads are blocked or contended—only the fuzzer main loop is [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimpacted.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code areas to investigate  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  To obtain a holistic understanding of the hang, review:  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Apache FontBox’s Type1 font parser, especially `readEncoding`, `parseASCII` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand the generic `parse` loop.  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. The PFB-based font creation path in `Type1Font.createWithPFB`.  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. PDFBox font factory and resource resolution: `PDFontFactory.createFont` and [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`PDResources.getFont`.  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. The text-extraction engine call sequence in `SetFontAndSize.process` → [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`PDFStreamEngine.processOperator` → `PDFTextStripper.processPage`.  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. The fuzzer harness entry point [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`PDFExtractTextFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, to[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munderstand how input is fed into the parsing pipeline [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthough the harness itself is[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnot the root cause[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
